## Section 021: Retry Backpressure Guidance
### Question 01: What decision does this reference help make?
- **current_section_observation:** Section 021 "Retry Backpressure Guidance", Question 01 on governing decision: the seed currently shows that the seed corpus-process bullets stand beside this file's runtime gate, four verify lines covering blocking work on executors, locks across await, cancellation and timeout handling, and secret logging, the family's async safety kernel recast as reviewable checks, each verify line a gate-shaped restatement of an entrypoint avoid-line
- **supporting_reason:** Section 021 "Retry Backpressure Guidance", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision matters because the entrypoint says avoid while this file says verify, the same doctrine at two pipeline positions, prevention during design and detection during review, so the bundle encodes its async rules twice by phase, the load-order redundancy pattern applied to safety content
